__How to book profits in our Trades..?✅

📈Many of you are new here and don’t know how to book profits in a trade and mostly are always confused about TPs.
Coz sometimes trades hit all TPs some hit 2-3 TPs and sometimes trades only hit TP1.

➡️ So…Here are two methods that you can use with our signals, which always keep you in profits ✅

1. First is trailing SL method, you always have to trail SL with profits and with each TP it means just trail SL in profits or at entry after hit TP1 and keep trailing it with each TP…don’t try to hodl without trailing SL till last TP or you will end-up with loss in cases of reversals🔺

2. Second is booking whole position at TP1, Just close your entire position at TP1 without any Greed of further profits.
We follow proper risk management and our SLs very small which is just 20-30% with leverage and our TP1 is also same as SL, and SL hits are very rare in comparison of TP1 hit.
So you will be always in profits even if you close 100% position at TP1✅

Choose one of above methods with our signals and you will always in profits with our Signals🚀

Hopefully now you will not spam in  DM about Hitting SL after TP hits🙂

Regards Admin__ ❤️

- Funding high on futures and over leverage, so a reset cleans out the excess

- Profit takers who brought early
